[09:38:09.926]                     }
[09:38:09.926]                     else if (inherits(cond, "warning")) {
[09:38:09.926]                       muffled <- grepl(pattern, "muffleWarning")
[09:38:09.926]                       if (muffled)

[09:38:09.926]                         for (restart in restarts) {
[09:38:09.926]                           name <- restart$name
[09:38:09.926]                           if (is.null(name)) 
[09:38:09.926]                             next
[09:38:09.926]                           if (!grepl(pattern, name)) 
[09:38:09.926]                             next
[09:38:09.926]                           invokeRestart(restart)
[09:38:09.926]                           muffled <- TRUE
[09:38:09.926]                           break
[09:38:09.926]                         }
[09:38:09.926]                       }
[09:38:09.926]                     }
[09:38:09.926]                     invisible(muffled)
[09:38:09.926]                   }
